# WOCE temperature section

## (with multiple colormaps)

<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[1]:
</div>

```python
import iris

iris.FUTURE.netcdf_promote = True

url = 'http://icdc.cen.uni-hamburg.de/thredds/dodsC/ftpthredds/woce/wghc_params.nc'

cubes = iris.load_raw(url)
```

<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[2]:
</div>

```python
print(cubes)
```
<div class="output_area"><div class="prompt"></div>
<pre>
    0: Silicate / (micromole/kg)           (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    1: Sig2 / (kg/m3)                      (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    2: Oxygen / (micromole/kg)             (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    3: Salinity / (1)                      (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    4: Sig0 / (kg/m3)                      (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    5: Nitrate / (micromole/kg)            (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    6: Sig4 / (kg/m3)                      (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    7: Tpoten / (degrees C)                (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    8: Bot_Dep / (m)                       (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    9: Phosph / (micromole/kg)             (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    10: Pres / (decibars)                   (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    11: Gamman / (kg/m3)                    (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)
    12: Temp / (degrees C)                  (ZAX: 44; latitude: 341; longitude: 720)

</pre>
</div>
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[3]:
</div>

```python
tpoten = cubes.extract_strict('Tpoten')
sig0 = cubes.extract_strict('Sig0')
```

<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[4]:
</div>

```python
tpoten = tpoten.extract(
    iris.Constraint(longitude=lambda cell: 334 <= cell < 334.5)
)

sig0 = sig0.extract(
    iris.Constraint(longitude=lambda cell: 334 <= cell < 334.5)
)

y = tpoten.coord(axis='Y').points
z = tpoten.coord(axis='Z').points
```

<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[5]:
</div>

```python
%matplotlib inline
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from oceans.colormaps import cm

cmap = cm.odv

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(19, 7.25))
cs = ax.pcolormesh(y, z, tpoten.data, cmap=cmap)
ax.set_ylim(0, 2000)
ax.set_xlim(-60, 60)
ax.invert_yaxis()
ax.set_ylabel('depth (m)')
ax.set_xlabel('latitude (degrees)')

fig.colorbar(cs, orientation='vertical', shrink=0.95, fraction=0.15, extend='both')

levels = [24.5, 25, 26, 26.5, 27, 27.5]
clabel = ax.contour(y, z, sig0.data, colors='w', levels=levels)
ax.clabel(clabel, fmt=r'%.1f')
```

```python
import palettable

cmap = palettable.cmocean.sequential.Thermal_9.mpl_colormap
```

<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[7]:
</div>

```python
fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(19, 7.25))
cs = ax.pcolormesh(y, z, tpoten.data, cmap=cmap)
ax.set_ylim(0, 2000)
ax.set_xlim(-60, 60)
ax.invert_yaxis()
ax.set_ylabel('depth (m)')
ax.set_xlabel('latitude (degrees)')

fig.colorbar(cs, orientation='vertical', shrink=0.95, fraction=0.15, extend='both')

levels = [24.5, 25, 26, 26.5, 27, 27.5]
clabel = ax.contour(y, z, sig0.data, colors='w', levels=levels)
ax.clabel(clabel, fmt=r'%.1f')
```

</div>

```python
fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(19, 7.25))
cs = ax.pcolormesh(y, z, tpoten.data, cmap=cmap)
ax.set_ylim(0, 2000)
ax.set_xlim(-60, 60)
ax.invert_yaxis()
ax.set_ylabel('depth (m)')
ax.set_xlabel('latitude (degrees)')

fig.colorbar(cs, orientation='vertical', shrink=0.95, fraction=0.15, extend='both')

levels = [24.5, 25, 26, 26.5, 27, 27.5]
clabel = ax.contour(y, z, sig0.data, colors='w', levels=levels)
ax.clabel(clabel, fmt=r'%.1f')
```
